The sequence of how to express A in German Sign Language is as follows:
1. Extend your index finger and thumb, touching the tips together
2. Bring your hand down slightly in a quick motion
3. Relax your hand and bring it back up to the starting position

The sequence of how to express A+Z in German sign language is as follows.
1. Hold your dominant hand in the 'A' handshape, palm facing up.
2. Bring your non-dominant hand up to the side of your dominant hand, in the 'Z' handshape, palm facing inwards.
3. Rotate your non-dominant hand so that the palm faces outward, parallel to your dominant hand.
4. Close both hands into fists simultaneously.

2. Bring the index finger down to the chin. 
3. Move the hand in a small circle in front of the chest. 
4. Tap the chest with the index finger.

The sequence of how to express AB in German sign language is as follows:
1. Extend both arms forward, palms facing down.
2. Bring both hands back towards the body, palms facing up.

4. Extend both arms out to the sides, palms facing up.
5. Bring both hands back towards the body, palms facing up.
6. Cross both hands in front of the chest, left hand over right.

2. Rotate hands outward as if holding a basket and gather imaginary items.
3. Lift hands upward as if presenting the harvested items.
4. Finish with hands in a closed fist, mimicking the action of storing the harvest.

The sequence of how to express ERSCHROCKEN in German Sign Language is as follows:
1. Start with hands in front of chest, fingers spread out.
2. Move hands outwards quickly, fingers still spread, with a surprised expression on face.
3. Bring hands back to chest, close fingers together in a tight grip.
4. Raise shoulders slightly while keeping hands close to chest.
5. Open mouth slightly as if gasping in shock.
6. Lower hands back to sides slowly, with a look of fear on face.

The sequence of how to express ERST in German Sign Language is as follows. 
1. Start with both hands in a closed fist position in front of your chest
2. Open your hands and extend your index fingers outward
3. Bring your right index finger up to your mouth and touch your lips
4. Bring your right index finger down and tap your left wrist
5. Bring your left index finger up to your mouth and touch your lips
6. Bring your left index finger down and tap your right wrist

The sequence of how to express ERSTE in German sign language is as follows. 
1. Start with both hands at chest level, palms facing downward. 
2. Extend both hands forward and slightly upward, with fingers spread. 
3. Bring both hands back to chest level and close them into fists. 
4. Move both fists upward in a quick motion, then open them and hold them in front of your chest.

The sequence of how to express ERSTMAL in German sign language is as follows.
1. Start with hands open, palms facing up, in front of chest.
2. Move hands outward and downward in a sweeping motion.
3. Bring hands back to starting position.
4. Close hands into fists and bring them up to chest level, with thumbs touching shoulders.
5. Open hands and rotate them outward, away from the body.
6. Finish with hands open and palms facing forward, slightly tilted to the side.

The sequence of how to express ERWARTEN in German sign language is as follows.
1. Extend both hands in front of you, palms facing upwards.
2. Slowly bring both hands towards your chest in a cupping motion.
3. Tilt your head slightly to the side while maintaining the hand position.
4. Hold the hand position at chest level for a few seconds before releasing.

The sequence of how to express ERZ in German sign language is as follows.
1. Right hand fingerspelling the letters E-R-Z
2. Both hands forming the shape of a pickaxe swinging down
3. Head tilting slightly to the side as if observing a rock
4. Right hand mimicking the action of mining with a pickaxe
5. Both hands coming together to show the shape of a rock being broken apart
6. Head nodding in agreement as if discovering something valuable

2. Bring both hands together in front of chest, palms facing each other
3. Separate hands and move them to either side of the body
4. Rotate both hands outward while keeping palms facing forward.

3. Alternate raising and lowering your hands as if walking quickly.

3. Close both hands into fists at shoulder height.
4. Open both hands again, palms facing upwards.
5. Bring hands in towards the body, then outwards in a circular motion.
6. Finish with hands back at shoulder height, palms facing upwards.

1. Start with both hands in fists, palms facing down.
2. Extend both index fingers and thumbs.

8. Separate both hands apart, transitioning back into 'N' handshapes.
9. Finish by moving both hands outward and slightly upwards, while maintaining the 'N' handshapes.

The sequence of how to express REGION in German Sign Language is as follows. 
1. Start with hands in a closed position near the chest. 
2. Move hands outward and upward in a circular motion, mimicking the outline of a region on a map. 
3. Bring hands back together at the chest to symbolize the idea of a defined area. 
4. End with hands apart, emphasizing the concept of boundaries and territory.

The sequence of how to express REIF in German sign language is as follows. 
1. Start with both hands in fists, palms facing upwards. 
2. Bring both hands up to chest level, then extend fingers and twist hands outwards. 
3. Bring hands back to starting position and flick fingers outwards. 
4. Tilt head slightly downwards while keeping hands at chest level.

The sequence of how to express REIN in German sign language is as follows:
1. Start with both hands in fists, palms facing down.
2. Bring both hands up to shoulder height with fists still closed.
3. Open both hands and move them downward in a scooping motion.
4. Close both hands into fists again as they come back up to shoulder height.
5. Open both hands and spread fingers as if showing something small.
6. Move both hands forward and slightly downward in a gentle pushing motion.

The sequence of how to express REKORD in German sign language is as follows. 
1. Start with both hands in fists in front of you. 
2. Move arms outwards to the sides in a sweeping motion. 
3. Bring hands back together in front of you. 
4. Make a quick tapping motion with both hands in front of you.

The sequence of how to express REST in German sign language is as follows. 
1. Begin with hands pointed downwards, palms facing each other, with one hand slightly above the other. 
2. Bring the hands together, interlocking the fingers and then flipping them so that the back of one hand is resting on the palm of the other. 
3. Hold this position for a moment, symbolizing rest or relaxation. 
4. Slowly separate the hands and return them to the starting position.

The sequence of how to express RHEIN in German sign language is as follows. 
1. Start with both hands by your chest, palms facing each other. 
2. Move both hands outward and downward in a flowing motion, resembling the flow of a river. 
3. Finish the sign by bringing both hands back to your chest.

The sequence of how to express RHEIN-PFALZ in German Sign Language is as follows.
1. Start with both hands at chest level, fingers together pointing outward.
2. Separate hands, moving them in circular motions outward and then back in towards each other.
3. Bring hands together in front of chest, palms facing down, fingers pointing outwards.
4. Move hands down and outwards, repeating the circular motion.
5. Extend right hand forward, palm facing left, fingers pointing down.
6. Repeat the circular motion with the right hand, moving it in a circular motion to the right.

The sequence of how to express RHEINLAND in German sign language is as follows. 
1. Extend both hands forward in front of the chest, palms facing down. 
2. Move both hands in a circular motion, as if tracing the shape of a river. 
3. Bring both hands together in front of the chest, palms facing each other. 
4. Separate both hands outward, as if spreading apart.

The sequence of how to express RHEINLAND-PFALZ in German sign language is as follows:
1. Start with both hands forming the letter 'R' by placing the index and middle fingers of each hand together and pointing them upwards.
2. Move both hands downward and to the right in a smooth motion, as if tracing the outline of a river.
3. Transition into forming the letter 'P' by bending the middle and ring fingers of both hands and bringing them together in front of the chest.
4. Extend the pinky fingers of both hands outward to the sides, forming the letter 'F'.
5. Finally, bring both hands together in a slight clapping motion to complete the sign for RHEINLAND-PFALZ.

The sequence of how to express RICHTIG in German sign language is as follows. 
1. Start with both hands in a fist shape, palms facing down.
2. Bring both hands up towards the chest, opening them as if unfolding a book.
3. Move both hands outwards and upwards, mimicking the concept of correctness or accuracy.
4. Finish with both hands coming together in front of the chest, fingers pointing upwards.

The sequence of how to express RICHTUNG in German sign language is as follows. 
1. Point right index finger in the direction of the word.
2. Move hand in that direction in a straight line.
3. Bring hand back to starting position.
4. Repeat motion to emphasize direction.

The sequence of how to express RISIKO in German Sign Language is as follows:
1. Extend both hands out in front of you, palms facing down.
2. Bring both hands together and cross them in front of your body.
3. Extend your dominant hand out, palm facing down, while keeping your non-dominant hand at your side.
4. Make a slicing motion with your dominant hand, cutting across the palm of your non-dominant hand.
5. Move your dominant hand up and down in a bouncing motion, emphasizing the risky nature of the concept.

The sequence of how to express ROSTOCK in German Sign Language is as follows:
1. Index finger extended on dominant hand, pointing to the right
2. Non-dominant hand flat with palm facing up, moving in a circular motion
3. Dominant hand moves in a diagonal downward motion, fingers together
4. Non-dominant hand remains stationary, palm facing up
5. Dominant hand closes into a fist, with thumb on top

4. Open both hands again, palms facing up, at shoulder height.

4. Move both hands outward and downward simultaneously, extending arms.
5. Bring hands back to neutral position, palms facing down.
6. Shake head from side to side while keeping hands at chest level.

The sequence of how to express neg-NOCH-NICHT in German sign language is as follows. 
1. Hands start from neutral position by the chest, palms facing down. 
2. Hands move out in a diagonal motion to the sides, palms still facing down. 
3. Head tilts slightly to the left as hands move outwards. 
4. Both hands flip over so palms are facing up.

2. Move both hands upwards and to the left in a diagonal motion. 
3. Rotate both hands to face upwards, still in a negation movement. 
4. Tilt head slightly to the left while keeping hands in position.

2. Extend both index fingers and point them downwards.
3. Bring both hands towards the chest while moving them apart, indicating negation.
